\DoxyCodeLine{00328\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ decode\ the\ next\ frame\ and\ return\ the\ number\ of\ *samples*\ per\ channel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00329\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Note\ that\ for\ interleaved\ data,\ you\ pass\ in\ the\ number\ of\ shorts\ (the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00330\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ size\ of\ your\ array),\ but\ the\ return\ value\ is\ the\ number\ of\ samples\ per}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00332\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00333\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ data\ is\ coerced\ to\ the\ number\ of\ channels\ you\ request\ according\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00334\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ channel\ coercion\ rules\ (see\ below).\ You\ must\ pass\ in\ the\ size\ of\ your}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00335\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ buffer(s)\ so\ that\ stb\_vorbis\ will\ not\ overwrite\ the\ end\ of\ the\ buffer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00336\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ maximum\ buffer\ size\ needed\ can\ be\ gotten\ from\ get\_info();\ however,}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00338\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ per\ channel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00339\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{00345\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ M\ \ \ \ N\ \ \ \ \ \ \ output}}
